  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_23aadf70-f0e5-4dac-885e-48e09f3602ea'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText4827183082712588899" style="display:none"><b> <i>From New York Times Best-Selling Author K. Bromberg comes an unforgettable series about lust, love, redemption, and healing...</i></b><br /><br />Our paths should never have crossed.<br /><br />Colton Donavan was arrogant, exuded that bad boy vibe, and embodied everything I never wanted. And yet all it took was one night, one hallway, and one stolen kiss for me to know I hated him and desired him instantly.<br /><br />My heart was healing. His soul was damaged. But with one bid, one little boy, and one carnival date, I couldn’t walk away and he wouldn’t let me in.<br /><br />This is our story. Our fight. <i> Our perfectly imperfect love.</i><br /><br /><br />Longer description:<br /><br /><b>Rylee Thomas is used to being in control. But she’s about to meet the one man that just might make her enjoy losing it…</b><br /><br />I am the exception to the rule. <br /><br />In a world full of willing women, I’m a challenge to the roguish and achingly handsome Colton Donavan. A man used to getting exactly what he wants in all aspects of life. He’s the reckless bad boy constantly skating that razor thin edge toward out of control, on and off of the track. <br /><br />Colton crashes into my life like a tornado: sapping my control, testing my vulnerabilities beyond their limits, and unintentionally penetrating the protective wall around my healing heart. Tearing apart the world I rebuilt so carefully with structure, predictability, and discipline.<br /><br /><i>I can’t give him what he wants and he can’t give me what I need.</i> But after a glimpse beneath his refined exterior into the dark secrets of his damaged soul, can I bring myself to walk away?<br /><br />Our sexual chemistry is undeniable. Our individual need for complete control is irrefutable. But when our worlds collide, is the chemistry enough to bring us together or will our untold secrets and battle of wills force us apart?</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I bought the whole series, unfortunately, before being so totally turned off on that ass who is the hero. Colton, in THIS day and age, shouldn't even <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I bought the whole series, unfortunately, before being so totally turned off on that ass who is the hero. Colton, in THIS day and age, shouldn't even be written about. You don't use your past to justify bad behavior, abusive behavior. Then I made the mistake of watching the Passionflix series, or at least the part they made from the first book. Ugh. Rylee (I HATE it when cutesy 80's names are used, except in this case, suits her to a "T"), has no backbone, no strength, no nothing. Her personality falls flat and the fact that she lets him abuse her? I'm figuring Bromberg had to pay Passionflix to make a movie out of this, I know I just cancelled the Roku part of my subscription to Passionflix, solely because of this.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

What a mess.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836168.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story is absolutely ridiculous.   <span id="freeText14711531627957646345" style="display:none"><b>*BR with Alex. We should do it more often ;-)* </b><br><br>You've got to be kidding me? Couldn't even finish, gave up at 43%. What a mess.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836168.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is absolutely ridiculous. We get yet another stupid thing falling out of some place and bumping into her prince charming. Can any of them walk a straight line anymore? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836169.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First there was Anna who fell into Christian's office, looked up and there he was. Then there was Eva who ran into Gideon, fell to her knees spilling her purse, looked up and there he was. Don't forget Catherine who caught the toe of her boot on a jagged edge and stubbled forward, right into William's arms. This time you get Rylee who falls out of a freaking closet, looks up and there he is, Colton. F@cking hell!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421097i/836170.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At 2% main characters were already sucking each others faces off. They just looked at each other and next thing you know, there is saliva splashing all over the place. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836171.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's oh-so-good, there are rainbows everywhere and unicorns flying around, somewhere in the background angels are singing "Amazing grace". You get the picture. <br><blockquote>
  <b>I move my hands over the rasp of his unshaven jaw to the back of his neck and tug my fingers in the hair that curls over the top of his collar.<br>(...)<br>I'm drowning in the sensation of him, and yet I'm not willing to come up for the air I so desperately need.<br>(...)<br>My body is ready to consent to his request because I want this man too. I want to feel his weight on me, his bare skin sliding on mine.<br></b>
</blockquote><br>Then suddenly she snaps out of it and gets all up in his face. <br><blockquote>
  <b>"Who the hell do you think you are? Touching me like that? Taking advantage of me that way?"<br></b>
</blockquote><br>WTF??!!! Come again???!!!!! I was expecting two nurses to jump out at any moment, one holding a straight jacked and the other one syringe with a sedative, to take Rylee back to where she escaped from.<br><br>From that point on all of their encounters were about her calling him a dick, arrogant prick, and accusing him of taking advantage of an innocent girl. I wasn't sure what girl she was referring to, because the chick that felt out of the closet wasn't it.<br><br>She says he is full of sh!t, but so is she. At least he was honest about it, I can't say the same about her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836172.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everytime he comes up with some kinky proposition she is all: who do you think I am, some slut? <br><blockquote>
  <b>I suppress my anger at the nerve of Colton. I can't believe he's just said this.</b>
</blockquote><br>But 2 seconds later, there are all kinds weird thing happening in her crotch area.<br><blockquote>
  <b>I watch his eyes narrow as I lick my lips. for all of a sudden it is rather hot in this conference room.</b>
</blockquote><br>He buys her at the auction, well, not her, but a date with her. It's not as kinky as it sounds. It's all for a good cause, because money will go to charity. While Christian Grey is trying to cure worlds hunger, Colton is trying to save orphans. Good for you, dude! But she, good girl that she is *eye roll*, feels like a whore, or a cheep slut, that have been put on a display and sold like some sex slave. No one is asking you to spread your legs, jeeze, relax! Just meet the dude, have a cup of coffee, laugh it off and move on. But no, she goes on an on about how humiliating it was. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421097ra/836173.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wanted to DNF this book 5% into it, but I kept reading because I wanted to see if Colton could walk the walk. You see, he kept promising her mind blowing orgasms.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Just know, Rylee, the best sex you will ever have... will be with me." He says in a low, hypnotizing voice.</b>
</blockquote><br>But when we finally got to see him in action, all you got was: yeah, that's it, oh god, look at me, that's right. <br>Rylee was in seven heaven, saw stars and the whole shebang. From where I was reading, it was "Meh" at best. Apparently, Rylee gets off on clichés.<br><br>That's all I have. Wasn't good, at all. Not even close to being mediocre in my opinion. </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610753747?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610753747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9829600955223440381"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/BlombergDrivenTitlebySueBee_zps8ad4b29c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420901i/835515.jpg' alt=' photo BlombergDrivenTitlebySueBee_zps8ad4b29c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★! The Driven Trilogy, book 1, a Debut by K. Blomberg. Famous, rich, sexy & unattainable playboy & race car driver Colton Donavan’s fast and furious pursuit of broken and withdrawn regular girl, Rylee Thomas!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I will revel in that moment with him which will be filled with reverent sighs and entangled bodies, and I’ll be devastated when he walks away after having his fill of me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Driven Trilogy is the fast-paced whirlwind romance of an ordinary girl with a painful</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9829600955223440381" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/BlombergDrivenTitlebySueBee_zps8ad4b29c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420901i/835515.jpg" alt=" photo BlombergDrivenTitlebySueBee_zps8ad4b29c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★! The Driven Trilogy, book 1, a Debut by K. Blomberg. Famous, rich, sexy &amp; unattainable playboy &amp; race car driver Colton Donavan’s fast and furious pursuit of broken and withdrawn regular girl, Rylee Thomas!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I will revel in that moment with him which will be filled with reverent sighs and entangled bodies, and I’ll be devastated when he walks away after having his fill of me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Driven Trilogy is the fast-paced whirlwind romance of an ordinary girl with a painful past, Rylee Thomas</b>, working for a non-profit organization when her world collides with the beyond handsome, elusive and jaded, (in)famous playboy, sought after bachelor and successful race car driver with Hollywood family ties, <b>Colton Donavan</b>. After meeting at a fundraiser Colton sets out on a relentless seduction and chase of Rylee. <b>Fasten your seatbelts to follow them in their saga spanning three books.</b><br><br><u>Books in The Driven Trilogy should be read in order:</u><br><b>Driven (book 1)<br>Fueled (book 2) – due August 2013<br>Crashed (book 3)</b><br><br><b>Driven (book 1) opens up with Rylee’s and Colton’s first encounter</b> backstage at a fundraiser that she is organizing and he is attending. <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I freeze instantly, shocked at the audacity of our party’s attendees, when I hear the unmistakable sound of a zipper followed by a breathless but familiar feminine gasp of, “Oh yes!” in the darkened alcove a few feet in front of me.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>Before the night is over Rylee finds herself rescued, kissed, insulted, pursued, tempted, coerced and ultimately obligated to a date thanks to a donation paid for by Colton Donavan. Needless to say they are off to a bumpy start. <br><br>Rylee is very broken with a tragic past and she will fight his seduction every step of the way. Colton however is used to getting what he wants and “Driven” is his middle name. Her resistance only serves to fuel his determination. He ends up making a huge contribution to Corporate Cares and Rylee finds herself working side-by-side with Colton on the project.<br><br>Their attraction and sexual tension are palpable, but both are strong-willed and with an innate need for control. And Colton also has demons which he is determined to keep to himself. Add to that vindictive exes and the scrutinizing spotlight by the media and <b>we have a story filled with intrigue and suspense, secrets and demons, twists and turns, villains and set-backs.</b><br><br>Colton’s and Rylee’s story moves along a break-neck speed only to come to a crashing halt with a cliff-hanger ending. I am not too worried as August is right around the corner plus there was a teaser for book 2, Fueled at the end.<br><br>With Driven’s cliff-hanger ending, lots of loose ends and unanswered questions it is <b>my prediction for the rest of The Driven Trilogy there’ll be plenty of more drama and intrigue added to keep us guessing and fretting all the way to the finish line.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He turns to go, but not before I watch the transition on his face from the Colton Donavan I know, to the public persona. Aloof and untouchable. Sexy and untamable.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/BlombergDriven1HerobySueBee_zpsc234da20.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420901i/835516.jpg" alt=" photo BlombergDriven1HerobySueBee_zpsc234da20.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Colton Donavan has everything I could ever ask for in a hero</b> with his larger-than-life personality, movie star good looks and sex appeal. From Hollywood royalty he grew up determined to make it on his own by becoming a successful race car driver and business man. The word no does not exist in his vocabulary. He is driven and relentless, in control yet out-of-control. Colton is also elusive and very much the unattainable playboy and sought after bachelor with a string of vindictive exes. But Colton also has secrets and a past which will unfold throughout the series so that maybe we will <b>better understand the enigma that is Colton Donavan.</b><br><br>I might have wished he’d remained aloof and suave a little longer in his seduction. As much as I love his intense personality, some of the dialogue felt off; His. Words. Were. Too. Excessive. Too. Soon. and some reminded me of other popular heroes. <b>However, I already saw huge progress in the last two-thirds of the book</b> and my wish for the next-coming books is that he continues on the hot and cold path plus improves his dialogue.<br><br>Six words to describe <b>Colton Donavan: Driven, charismatic, enigmatic, relentless, unattainable and broken.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I know all about baggage, sweetheart. I have enough of it to fill up a 747 and then some.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/BlombergDriven1HeroinebySueBee_zps3a005280.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420901i/835517.jpg" alt=" photo BlombergDriven1HeroinebySueBee_zps3a005280.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The greater the hero the tougher it is for the heroine to stand-out. I had a hard time connecting with <b>Rylee Thomas</b> at first. I found her difficult and complicated. <b>But as the story unfolds we learn more about her tragic and painful past, which is mitigating. Plus I applaud her for diving into and dealing with some of her issues.</b> Just like with Colton I saw a stark improvement in the second two-thirds of the story. My wish is for continued growth and less use of Colton’s nick-name “Ace”.<br><br>Six words to describe <b>Rylee Thomas: Complicated, damaged, caring, stubborn, progressive and endearing.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Sorry, sweetheart,” he murmurs, “you’re going to learn that sometimes, not being in control is extremely liberating.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><i>To explain my varying story execution rating: <b>This is a debut novel and when story is good it’s great, way on its way to a 5-star read and Colton at his best is up there with my favorite heroes.</b> But then there are moments that I touched on above, mostly in the first third of the book, where the dialogue feels a little off plus the story is long-winded.</i><br><br><b>An excellent debut by Ms. Blomberg! Interesting setting and plot! Refreshing storytelling! Captivating hero with HUGE potential! A very promising series!</b> I am looking forward to book 2, Fueled. Thanks Ms. Blomberg!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I know it won’t be enough. I don’t think any amount of time will be enough to love someone like Colton. He is one of those guys who consumes every part of you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4.5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storyline execution rating: 3.5-5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 4.5 stars<br>Story ending rating: N/A<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 3 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS/tumblr_luiha40xAU1qmzq91o1_500_zps9f2558d2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420901ra/835518.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_luiha40xAU1qmzq91o1_500_zps9f2558d2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=hero-asshat">hero-asshat</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer859756588" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9804054356027628571"><br/><b>1 'LOGIC FAIL AHEAD!' star</b> <br/><br/>Gaaahhhh!! I hate Alpha Jerks with CHEESY lines, and the doormat women who swoon over them! This was almost a DNF so many times, but I actually finished it. Maybe because it was such a train wreck, I actually found myself wondering just how fucked up these two really are. The answer? THEY ARE SERIOUSLY FUCKED UP. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394126824i/8811663.gif' alt='' width='370' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>FIRST, MEET COLTON:</b> <br/>He is the typical misogynist A-hole alpha-jerk hero who believes himself too damaged for love, so he commits to sex-only relationships. He</span>
  <span id="freeText9804054356027628571" style="display:none"><br><b>1 'LOGIC FAIL AHEAD!' star</b> <br><br>Gaaahhhh!! I hate Alpha Jerks with CHEESY lines, and the doormat women who swoon over them! This was almost a DNF so many times, but I actually finished it. Maybe because it was such a train wreck, I actually found myself wondering just how fucked up these two really are. The answer? THEY ARE SERIOUSLY FUCKED UP. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394126824i/8811663.gif" alt="" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>FIRST, MEET COLTON:</b> <br>He is the typical misogynist A-hole alpha-jerk hero who believes himself too damaged for love, so he commits to sex-only relationships. He has an endless supply of cheesy one liners, brags constantly about his cock size and prowess in bed, has no problems with sloppy-seconds, sends mixed signals til you go crazy, and has some seriously creepy stalker tendencies.<br><br>COLTON ONLY DOES THE SEX THING, NO EMOTIONS OR RELATIONSHIPS. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392735925i/8603003.jpg" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>COLTON DECIDES WHAT HIS WOMEN WANT FROM HIM AND WHEN:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393709345ra/8755136.gif" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>COLTON IS AN ENDLESS LIBRARY OF CHEESY, SMARMY PICKUP LINES!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393713937i/8755722._SX540_.png" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>COLTON GETS ALL OF HIS WOMEN BY BEING AN ASS, AND THEY LOVE IT!: <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393705926i/8754845.png" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>NOW, MEET RYLEE:</b><br>Our doormat extraordinaire heroine who piles on the excuses for Colton's asshole behavior, says one thing but always does another, spreads her legs at his commands, and believes she can fix this dude because she is sooooo special. Why does she bother? <b>
  <i>BECAUSE HE IS SO HOT!! </i>
</b> (eye roll!)<br><br>RYLEE MAY SAY SHE WANTS CONTROL, BUT HER ACTIONS ARE PURE DOORMAT<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393723301i/8756845._SX540_.jpg" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>COLTON CONTINUES TO MAKE HER CRY, AND YET RYLEE GOES BACK FOR MORE AND MORE...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381959938ra/5476130.gif" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SHE EMBRACES HER 'INNER SLUT', WHICH COLTON IS ALL TOO HAPPY TO TAKE ADVANTAGE OF:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393723753i/8756880.png" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, she REALLY has an inner slut. It is what her and her friend chat about, and it gives her the excuse to behave like a doormat with Colton. She tries to convince herself that she can do 'sex only', despite never doing it before, and (no surprise!) she can't do it. She gets emotionally attached (again, no surprise!) Which is why she cries and breaks down so often. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394135785ra/8812565.gif" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is book 1 in a series, so there is no HEA nor do we get all of the answers as why they are so fucked up. There are hints of what has him so emotionally closed up, how her fiance died, and what A.C.E. stands for. But honestly, I don't really care anymore. This series did not work for me. It ends as expected, with Colton being a fucking douche bag. We already know Rylee can't resist him being an asshole to her, so of course she will take him back a few dozen more times.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394146090ra/8813832.gif" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a formula that many books are using these days, i.e. asshole hero + doormat heroine + a shit load of fighting over his inability to commit. I am not a person who believes that 'Severe Asshole Syndrome' can be fixed by some great sex with an airhead who should have ran for the hills when they first met. So, I am done with this series. Moving on...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421164i/836364.jpg" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393724209i/8756914._SX540_.jpg" width="370" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText17761909507369243566" style="display:none"><b>5 AH-MAZING Stars*****</b><br><br>OMG what a Ride.... I don't know why its taken me so long to read this series, I'm telling you if you haven't just like me then STOP EVERYTHING and meet ACE!!!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/730738DC-BF2C-4E4D-A3B6-453CE959DB3C_zpsns6f9fv1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I'm not going to write a big review as planning to do a series review at the end, but here are some of my thoughts so far. <br><br><b>Sigh and swoon.</b> what I have loved so far about this book is how Kristy has made palpable characters that give us feelings of realism. You literally feel and need to know what it's like to be <b>THEM</b> so much so you feel like your intruding in a way to there life. Except you can't help but keep watching it move forward, you can see it happened and know it's shifting yet you keep on because you see their souls unravel.<br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/E489D090-EE09-417F-A050-07BFFF5F3DC6_zpsx5ncmsul.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>In this book/series we are dealing with an emotional back story, that tore my heart open <b>NO JOKE.</b> Spoke to me in volumes. <br><br><b>Colton</b><br>Dominating, sensual, endearing in ways because he doesn't quite see it for himself. Yet he is able to connect and help the people around him, he loves easily except he's hurting on the inside. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/49A31EC1-EC63-447A-A18B-269822134661_zpsi4hpyev7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>Rylee</b><br>KICKASS heroine. Love her to bits, strong and giving at the same time.<br><br>I just love the writing and the message the story tells, the sex is HOT yet the story envelopes you. <br><br>Unputtadownable!! <div id="review_624036257" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/624036257" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/624036257?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer624036257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7368877210747920421"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393096365i/8661318._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392937164i/8636540._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>^^^ my casting for Colton </i><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br/><br/><strong>Well, I'm officially in love with Colton Donavan and hooked on this series!</strong><br/><br/>I'd been looking forward to starting this series for quite a while now. Honestly, I'd loved the sound it from the day I first heard about it but because of the cliffhangers, I was waiting to be able to read them all at once. Now that I've started it though, I totally get why so many readers are obsessed with these books! <br/><br/>The story followed Colton and Rylee. Rylee was</span>
  <span id="freeText7368877210747920421" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393096365i/8661318._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392937164i/8636540._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>^^^ my casting for Colton </i><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br><br><strong>Well, I'm officially in love with Colton Donavan and hooked on this series!</strong><br><br>I'd been looking forward to starting this series for quite a while now. Honestly, I'd loved the sound it from the day I first heard about it but because of the cliffhangers, I was waiting to be able to read them all at once. Now that I've started it though, I totally get why so many readers are obsessed with these books! <br><br>The story followed Colton and Rylee. Rylee was a strong woman who had control over life and who dedicated her time towards working for a wonderful cause helping children in need. Colton was a reckless bad boy -- a famous race car driver known for his skills both on the track and in the bedroom. They were polar opposites in so many ways and what she needed was something he couldn't give.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>“Let’s face it, you’re not a spend the night kind of guy, and I’m not a one-night stand kind of girl.” </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And yet, they kept being drawn back to each other... :)<br><br>I loved Rylee right from the start. She was a feisty, unintimidated and kind hearted. My first impression of Colton though was more of an arrogant, cocky manwhore... in Rylee's words, an "egotistical asshole". But I liked him! There was just something about him that hinted that there was much more to him than met the eye. Plus, he was just hot as hell!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I may be a man, but I'm nowhere near gentle. In fact, I think you're a little curious just how I like it. Step over the edge with me, Ryles…I'll be anything and everything but gentle."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>As Rylee soon found out, there <em>was</em> a lot more to him. Behind the bad boy that the world saw was deep rooted pain from a very dark past that he didn't want to talk about. I really felt drawn to his character. What can I say, I'm a total sucker for the tortured bad boys. They get to me every time.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"The man is captivating in every way and the epitome of sexy. From that boyish grin that disarms me in seconds to his sexy swagger… He exudes virility, evokes desire, and commends attention… He's edgy and reckless and you want to go along for the ride hoping to get a glimpse of his tender side that breaks through every now and again. The bad boy with a touch of vulnerability who leaves you breathless and steals your heart."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Colton was dominant and possessive. He knew what he wanted and was determined to get it no matter what. But he kept his heart locked away. He was used to purely physical relationships with women, and was simply not ready to commit to anything more.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I assure you, romance is not something I actively subscribe to. There's no such thing as happily ever after."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>What I loved was that Rylee brought out a new side of him he'd never allowed to show through before -- she meant more to him than anyone had before and that scared him. I loved the two sides of him -- on one hand he was cocky and arrogant, but he also had a deeply caring side. It was the side of him he hid from the world that drew me to him. I could feel how much he <em>wanted</em> "more" and it broke my heart that he didn't think he could ever have it.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I know all about baggage, sweetheart. I have enough of it to fill up a 747 and then some... </em>
    <em>My shit can't be fixed. I've been broken for way too long for that miracle to happen."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And I just want to share this line here because this was the moment that fully sold me on the series...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I'm seeing the true Colton Donavan - the unmasked version with a vulnerability that makes me want to reach over and take the hurt that often flickers through those green eyes and make it better. To show him that love and commitment are possible without complications. That it is real and pure and much more powerful than ever imagined with it is built and shared between two people."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Another part of the story I loved was that, as I mentioned, Rylee worked for an organization whose goal was to help orphaned children and she did these shifts at The House which was where many of them lived<em>. </em>On it's own, this part of the story was deeply emotional but guys, seeing Colton with these kids was just... WOW. My heart <em>melted -- </em>it was just so beautiful and moving!!!<br><br>I'm not going to lie though -- this book was a bit of a rough start for me for several reasons. But everyone kept telling me to hang in there because it got better and they were right!! It did get better and I'm so glad I stuck with it because now I'm hooked on this series!!<br><br>Ok - now there's something which I kind of <em>have</em> to mention here... *twists lips* ... ok -- I'm just going to say it: this book has several strong similarities to both Fifty Shades and Crossfire. I'm not going to list them because I'm not one to nit pick but you'll notice when you read it if, like me, you're a fan of those two series. But, here's the thing... take as a whole, the story is not the same and so, even though those elements made me a little uncomfortable while I was reading, my advice is to just overlook them. That's what I did.<br><br>I'd say that overall, my enjoyment of this book was a steady upward climb. There were a few stumbles along the way, a few cases of deja vu, but all in all, it got better and better as it went and now...<br><br><strong>I'm hooked, intrigued, and I want more!!</strong> Colton is very much the type of hero I most easily fall for --  tortured, mysterious, and a little bit dangerous, but protective, dominant and kind hearted. Rylee is the kind of strong heroine who I can respect. Overall, I liked the pacing of the story, I enjoyed watching Rylee and Colton try to figure out their relationship and I can't wait to see what comes next. I do wish certain scenes hadn't been quite as 'familiar' for me, but from what I hear, the next book blows this one out of the water and based on how the story in this book has been steadily getting better for me, I totally believe that.<br><br>I would absolutely recommend this book, but my advice is to be patient with it in the beginning. I'm glad I started it, really glad I stuck with it, and am now ready to dive straight into the next book.<br><br>PS - there is a <em>giant cliffhanger</em> at the end and I am so freaking glad I waited to read these books back to back because if I had read this without having the next book, I would have been pissed beyond all reason. But now that I have the next book ready to go, I'm just giddy with excitement to dive right into it :D<br><br>Here's my second casting pic for Colton ;)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392871624i/8625993.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7368877210747920421" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/716280316" />
    <a title="Amber Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose"><img alt="Amber Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1356721991p2/11143936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/716280316?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amber Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amber Rose" href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose">Amber Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11143936-amber-rose?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716280316" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16412893430803876160"><b> DNF at 45% </b> <br/><br/>First let me start off with this might work for others but not every book is for everyone. This simply did not work for me. I do not want to discourage others from reading this book. Just wanted to throw that out there. <br/><br/>I am starting to lose my focus when it comes to the same type of books over and over told into several different ways. Yeah I liked them when they first came out almost 2 years ago but I'm over the helpless girl falling over a rich handsome guy who she cannot underst</span>
  <span id="freeText16412893430803876160" style="display:none"><b> DNF at 45% </b> <br><br>First let me start off with this might work for others but not every book is for everyone. This simply did not work for me. I do not want to discourage others from reading this book. Just wanted to throw that out there. <br><br>I am starting to lose my focus when it comes to the same type of books over and over told into several different ways. Yeah I liked them when they first came out almost 2 years ago but I'm over the helpless girl falling over a rich handsome guy who she cannot understand why he makes her feel the way she does. <br><br><a href="http://s1287.photobucket.com/user/bauswella/media/amber%20b/blahblahblah-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436174ra/881506.gif" alt=" photo blahblahblah-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I read over and over that the room was heating up with lust, everything became motionless, it was just the two of them. <br><br><b> Seriously?? </b> <br><br>Those were just some of the reasons why this book did not work for me. <br><br>Also RyleE meets Colton they were already making out within 3 minutes of meeting each other. Then she stops and says she is not this type of girl. To me she is that type of girl. RyleE keeps giving me these mix emotions. It's either you want to be a big girl, and get your groove on, or stop with all these I want him, no I don't feelings because they are not cute at all. <br><br>One of the major turn offs for me was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Colton was kissing a girl when she walks by in the beginning of the book, then she fucking kisses him. Okay whatever if you like sloppy seconds. Then it happens again at the club. He had a girl hanging off his shoulder and she kissed him. Next thing you know their eyes meet and time just stops once again and they are grinning on each other dancing... UGH!!! This chick needs to get her shit together.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><b> Yeah.... </b> This is not my cup of tea, maybe 2 years ago but not any more.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <i>I sigh into the welcoming silence, grateful for the chance to escape, even if only momentarily, from the mindsuck of the meaningless conversations on the other side of the door.</i>
</b><br/><br/>That is the f</span>
  <span id="freeText13943050429088370244" style="display:none"><b>4.5 OH. FUCKING. MY. STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435112ra/878998.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435112ra/878999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My goal is to make you smile when reading this review, because I smiled so much in this book, my cheeks hurt!!!!</b><br><br>What are you doing right now?   <i>I sigh into the welcoming silence, grateful for the chance to escape, even if only momentarily, from the mindsuck of the meaningless conversations on the other side of the door.</i>
</b><br><br>That is the first sentence. I was sucked in from the beginning. <b>This author can WRITE!!!</b><br><br>The story is about Colton and Rylee. Both are broken. Both feel an undeniable, aching pull toward each other. They meet behind stage at a charity function, and their first meeting will take your breath away! Yes, this book is Panty-dropping hot! But it’s also sweet! There are so many <b>MOMENTS</b> in this book. You just have to read it!!!<br><br><b>My Colton:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800202i/665625._SY540_.jpg" alt=":)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Rogue. Rebel. Reckless.</i>
</b> Colton is a famous race car driver. He is a bad boy, and he knows it. The man can talk dirty. <b>
  <i>The man can fill out denim.</i>
</b> He had a rough childhood and was adopted when he was five. He is very mysterious about his past. He keeps Rylee at an emotional distance because he knows he is not able to love and doesn’t want to hurt her. <br><br><b>My Rylee:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800202i/665626._SY540_.jpg" alt="Goodreads | Beyond Shame (Beyond, #1) by Kit Rocha - Reviews, Discussion, Bookclubs, Lists" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rylee is a social worker in charge of The House, a home for 7 young boys who would be lost in the foster care system, if Rylee was not there to care for them. These moments with these boys are so endearing, you may have a few tears. <br><br>Rylee struggles with moving on, with guilt. She has already <b>loved and lost,</b> and she fears falling for a man who can just <b>
  <i>fuck ‘em and chuck ‘em.</i>
</b> She also keeps Colton at a distance because she is afraid of getting too close. She isn’t a crazy runner, but she keeps the walls up around her heart. Rylee leads with her head instead of her heart. She is a thinker and is constantly doubting her heart’s pull toward Colton.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435112i/879001.jpg" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love all of the <b>music references.</b> Colton and Rylee communicate through music sometimes by texting songs with lyrics they want to say, whether they are fun, serious, or just damn sexy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435112i/879002.jpg" alt="taylor swift - red" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>A slow, seductive ballet highlighted with breathy moans and panted whimpers.</i>
</b><br><br><b>WARNING: This book causes spontaneous melting!!</b><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="282" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435112ra/879003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I. Do. Not. Take. What’s. Not. Offered. And we both know, sweetheart, you offered,” he smirks. “Willingly.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>Can cotton candy be sexy?? Colton teaches us that it can!!!!</b><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="670" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435112i/879004._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I want to build you up nice and slow and sweet like you need. Push you to crash over that edge. And then I want to fuck you the way I need to. Fast and hard until you’re screaming my name.</i>
</b><br><br><b>ARE YOU SMILING YET?????</b><br><br>Yes, there is a major cliffy at the end of this book, but the next book is out already, so you can start this one now while I go read Fueled!!!<br><br><i>Thanks for the buddy read Irene and Rae!!!</i><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10826522043177923012"><b>DNF</b><br/>To be fair, I haven't given this a real shot...I only read about 25% of it. But this guy is just slaying me, and I keep cringing when he opens his overly sexual, cocky, condescending, egotistical, know-it-all mouth. I'm going to just give a few of my not so favorite quotes and move on to something I know I'll like. So, if you'd like a little taste, read on:<br/><br/>In order of appearance:<br/><b>"You're lucky I don't drag you back in that storage closet I found you in and take what you offered. Make you cry o</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10826522043177923012" style="display:none"><b>DNF</b><br>To be fair, I haven't given this a real shot...I only read about 25% of it. But this guy is just slaying me, and I keep cringing when he opens his overly sexual, cocky, condescending, egotistical, know-it-all mouth. I'm going to just give a few of my not so favorite quotes and move on to something I know I'll like. So, if you'd like a little taste, read on:<br><br>In order of appearance:<br><b>"You're lucky I don't drag you back in that storage closet I found you in and take what you offered. Make you cry out my name." He nips softly at my ear, and I have to stifle the uncontrollable moan of desire that threatens to escape. "To fuck you and get you out of my system. <u>Then move on.</u>"</b><br>Cuz nothing says sexy like knowing you're disposable....<br><br>______________________________________________<br><br><b>"Let's get something straight, (...) If I want you, I can and will have you, at any time and in anyplace, sweetheart."</b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392961300ra/8639802.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Keep in mind these quotes are all taking place on the very first night that they meet.<br><br>______________________________________________<br><br><b>"So that's what it will sound like?"<br>I open my eyes, confused at his comment, to see him regarding me with a bemused look on his ace. "What?" I bark, my response harsh like a curse.<br>"Those words, <i>Oh, God,"</i> he mimics me, reaching out and running a finger down the side of my face, "Now I know exactly how you'll sound when you say that while I'm buried deep inside of you."</b><br>The only time a guy can say "deep inside of you" and have me not laugh is if it's Third Eye Blind, serenading me. Just sayin'...these are things that are in romance novels but are so ridiculously cheesy. Who says that? And within hours of meeting? Come on.<br><br>______________________________________________<br><br><b>"I didn't say anything about bondage," he smirks, cutting me off. "But if that's your thing, Rylee, I'd be more than happy to oblige. I can teach you <i>the ropes</i>"</b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392961098ra/8639740.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Big gag. Bad pun.<br><br>______________________________________________<br><br>And last but not least:<br><b>"Why tie myself to just one woman when there are so many out there vyin for my attention?"<br>(...)<br>"You sure are full of yourself, aren't you Ace?"<br>He cocks his head and looks at me. "I can arrange that it be you who's full of me instead, if you'd like?"</b><br>My husband laughed his ass off when I read that to him. Puhlease!!! <br><br>______________________________________________<br><br>Suffice it to say, not only did I find this hero not sexy at all, I found him decidedly lame. There's a difference between cocky and confident. This guy acts like the high school jock who gets to be the big playah on campus. Time to grow up, buddy. And I fully admit that I'm sure he gets better over the course of the book/series. So I'll leave this one to those who like the cockamamie hero here. And to the heroine who I'm sure ends up adoring him! :D</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1117308435" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13165954292763035915"> <b>4 Fast Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>Rylee went through a pretty tragic event and never completely recovered from that. Until he had been adopted Colton also had a pretty tragic past. Neither of them wants to feel, because they both believe they doesn’t know how to do that anymore. <br/>Until their worlds collide, they both have to work together and everything changes. Colton wants her and she wants him back, but he’s an f1 racer, with more money that he can count and a sordid past that insists on not being forgotten, wh</span>
  <span id="freeText13165954292763035915" style="display:none"> <b>4 Fast Stars. </b>	<br><br>Rylee went through a pretty tragic event and never completely recovered from that. Until he had been adopted Colton also had a pretty tragic past. Neither of them wants to feel, because they both believe they doesn’t know how to do that anymore. <br>Until their worlds collide, they both have to work together and everything changes. Colton wants her and she wants him back, but he’s an f1 racer, with more money that he can count and a sordid past that insists on not being forgotten, which makes her hesitant about him. Until both of them can’t resist anymore which will change everything. So buckle in, people, this is going to be a sexy and bumpy ride! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419180873i/13007640._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can now see why so many mixed feelings about these books. It gives a “50 Shades” and “Crossfire” vibe and I understand why some people probably won’t like that. And the use of too.many.sentences.like.this is pretty annoying. Personally, I really liked. I’m all for the “broken alpha male who falls in love and doesn’t know how to deal with it” type. This book is intense, emotional, and with some angst and many drama because of the protagonists fight against their feelings. (Don’t you worry hard-romance fans, despite his lack of understanding of his own feelings, they are pretty clear to readers, through his gestures.). This was a very promising beginning and after this end, I really need to hop onto the next book! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> Rylee, despite some minor annoyances, it’s a pretty good heroine. She survived a very tragic event so it’s normal for her to be afraid and sometimes insecure. However she is fierce and she doesn’t give in every time the heroes does something stupid just because he gives her a sexy smile. You go, girl! If you love the broken alpha male type you’re going to love Colton. It’s endearing to see him trying to understand all these new feelings, and despite some agitations he brought me through the book, where I just wanted to slap him, it has impossible not to fall for him. And they tougher are explosive, so get ready for some really intense moments. <br> <b>Steam: </b><br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Death. Abuse… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cliffhanger. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_635614477" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/635614477?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=unfinished">unfinished</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer635614477" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15373540475091336408">Marked as DNF at 32%.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392832808i/8619086.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Just too many things went wrong for me with this one. Such a shame, as I was <i>so</i> damn excited to read this book and started it right now because I felt like I needed a sure thing, that I could almost guarantee I'd love.<br/><br/>However, the all too frequent and cringe-worthy grammatical errors, the cheesy dialogue, the unbelievable (not in a good way) storyline, the ridiculous first encounter, the whole sentences randomly in italics, the fact that both the hero and the heroine pissed </span>
  <span id="freeText15373540475091336408" style="display:none">Marked as DNF at 32%.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392832808i/8619086.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just too many things went wrong for me with this one. Such a shame, as I was <i>so</i> damn excited to read this book and started it right now because I felt like I needed a sure thing, that I could almost guarantee I'd love.<br><br>However, the all too frequent and cringe-worthy grammatical errors, the cheesy dialogue, the unbelievable (not in a good way) storyline, the ridiculous first encounter, the whole sentences randomly in italics, the fact that both the hero and the heroine pissed me off, the creepy innuendos and the fact that it felt like the entire romance industry had thrown up on these pages, cramming every romance cliché in existence into the story, just made it impossible for me to connect with this book in any way.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384287172i/6837635.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The fact I only got through 30% of this book, in two days, speaks volumes. I just found it a struggle and kept putting it down. I was reading on the train and I mindlessly read two whole pages before I realised I hadn't taken in a word that I'd read and was listening to the conversation between a mother and daughter in the seat next to me, instead.<br><br>The heroine really irritated me. I don't know who I disliked more, him or her. First she was Miss Prim and Proper, then seconds later they were making out, then she was pulling away, then he was virtually sexually harassing her, then she was angry, then he was stalking her, then he stalked her some more at work and then because of one little thing she was all googly eyed over him... WTF?! *head spin* <br><br>The ghastly innuendos made me gag...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Hell hasn't frozen over yet. I'll let you know when it does."<br>He takes a step closer to me, his voice just above a whisper, "It seems you know all about being cole, Rylee. Why stay frigid when you know I can heat you up?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Bleurgh!<br><br>And I'm the first to admit to loving a confident, alpha male... but there is a line and for me, Colton leapt over the confident line into unattractive arrogance. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Just know, Rylee, the best sex you will ever have... will be with me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I told you you wouldn't be able to resist me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And then there were things that just didn't make any sense and felt poorly planned and thought out. For example, Colton is a celebrity racing driver. But Rylee didn't know who he was at first. She didn't recognise him even after she'd snogged his face off at her work function. Yet then the author writes things like this...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"And how would you know what I always have on my arm?"<br>How do I know that? Do I admit to him I occasionally glance through Haddie's subscription of People and roll my eyes at the ridiculous commentary? Do I confess that peruse Perezhilton.com as a distraction when I'm in the office sometimes.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>So she reads enough gossip rags to know about the women Colton has on his arm, but she doesn't know what he looks like?? It's a small error but it's just one example of how things didn't fit into place.<br><br>I felt like I was reading a totally different book to the <i>Driven</i> everybody recommended to me and raved about. I really wanted to fall in love with Colton Donavon. But sadly, I just didn't.<br><br>I hate it so much when that happens. :'(<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392832808i/8619087.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15373540475091336408" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9688605837555396992">I hate to say this but I dnf'ed at 68%.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420667ra/834741.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I just wasn't feeling it anymore. It started off really well, don't get me wrong this book is seriously well written and there is some extensive character development with some angst thrown in. But unfortunately it just wasn't enough for me. <br/><br/>I felt it was drawn out, I didn't like the heroine, Some of her behavior I understood but she had some serious self esteem issues. I mean everyone was a threat including her best friend. One minute she's sure of herself</span>
  <span id="freeText9688605837555396992" style="display:none">I hate to say this but I dnf'ed at 68%.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420667ra/834741.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just wasn't feeling it anymore. It started off really well, don't get me wrong this book is seriously well written and there is some extensive character development with some angst thrown in. But unfortunately it just wasn't enough for me. <br><br>I felt it was drawn out, I didn't like the heroine, Some of her behavior I understood but she had some serious self esteem issues. I mean everyone was a threat including her best friend. One minute she's sure of herself the next she's comparing herself to every woman out there. She needed constant reminder of how beautiful she is, and I understand why, it's just that the confidence that she periodically exuded didn't gel with basket case she was most of the time.<br><br>Now I understand not everyone likes reading the same thing, so in no way am I saying don't read this book. Reading is a very personal thing and we can't all agree on the same stuff. This book reeled me in, but somewhere along the line I lost that connection.</span>

</i>. I got <b>
  <i>ALPHA MALE</i>
</b>.<br><br>...and what a <i>fine specimen of alpha</i> *sigh*<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393177856i/8672581._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380353565ra/706927.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm so glad that I have the 2nd book already on my kindle because it ends - <i>**I know**</i> like all <b>
  <i> these kinds of books</i>
</b> - with a huge cliffhanger! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390927224ra/8299136.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10394383951171260736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_605568910" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/605568910" />
    <a title="J" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10343430-j"><img alt="J" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/605568910?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J" href="/user/show/10343430-j">J</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10343430-j?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer605568910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11752811934340307479"><br/><br/><b>IT'S LIVE ON AMAZON..... </b><br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Driven-The-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00CRMX26I/ref=sr_1_1ie=UTF8&qid=1368496900&sr=8-1&keywords=Driven+by+K.+Bromberg'>http://www.amazon.com/Driven-The-Tril...</a><br/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Full review now posted!!!!</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br/><br/><br/><b> Oh my HOLY. FREAKING. GOODNESS. THIS. BOOK. IS.... BEYOND. AMAZING. </b><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i> I'm still trying to catch my breath... Man is this book AWESOME!! </i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><br/>The story is told from the perspective of Rylee Thomas. <br/>26 yr. old Rylee works for Corporate Cares, a company that houses orphans. The state turns over their guardianship to her company. Corporate Care, houses kids who are at an age that the chance of adop</span>
  <span id="freeText11752811934340307479" style="display:none"><br><br><b>IT'S LIVE ON AMAZON..... </b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Driven-The-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00CRMX26I/ref=sr_1_1ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1368496900&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=Driven+by+K.+Bromberg">http://www.amazon.com/Driven-The-Tril...</a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Full review now posted!!!!</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br><br><b> Oh my HOLY. FREAKING. GOODNESS. THIS. BOOK. IS.... BEYOND. AMAZING. </b><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i> I'm still trying to catch my breath... Man is this book AWESOME!! </i>
</b><br><br><br><br>The story is told from the perspective of Rylee Thomas. <br>26 yr. old Rylee works for Corporate Cares, a company that houses orphans. The state turns over their guardianship to her company. Corporate Care, houses kids who are at an age that the chance of adoptions are pretty low. So instead of foster care, they have a home to live in, they have consistency of guardians, rules, school and counselling. <br><br>Rylee meets Colton Donavan backstage at her work function charity auction, after getting trapped in the storage closet, Rylee starts to panic when Colton saves the day. <br>They share an instant attraction, but in the heat of the moment, Rylee realises that the man that has her body pinned up against him, was only minutes ago engaged in a rendezvous with another woman.<br><br>Not impressed with the "Fuck em and Chuck em" game that Colton plays, Rylee will have no part in falling at Colton's feet. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> ~"What? Didn't you know that I happened upon you and your first conquest of the evening in the little alcove backstage?"<br>Donavan's eyes widen at my words. I continue, enjoying the surprised look on his face. <br>"Did she play you at your own game, Ace, and leave you wanting more? Aching to prove what a man you are since you couldn't fulfil her? That you had to pick a frantic woman locked in a closet to take advantage of? I mean, really how many women have you used your bullshit lines on tonight? How many have you tried to leave your mark on?"~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It was refreshing to have a heroine who was not afraid to speak her mind, not fall to the feet of this adonis that was Colton. <br>By the end of the night, Colton has secured a date with Rylee after bidding on her in the charity date auction. A date that, Rylee, has no intention of going to. <br><br><br>Colton, <i> Sigh</i> <br>Beautiful, damaged, Colton.<br>Hot and upcoming Race Car driver extraordinaire, son of a mega Hollywood- movie director and CEO of CD Enterprises. <br><br>Not having any control over Rylee is what initially attracts him the most to her. <br>Her resistance messes with him, intensifying his growing need to 'Fuck her, get her out of his system. Then move on.' <br>He just won't accept that this woman who responded to him in the heat of the moment, refuses to take it any further. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"Why stay frigid when you know I can heat you up?"~ Colton</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really did loved how she keeps him on his toes throughout the book, never quite giving into his pull, always making him work for it. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"You're so sure of yourself, do I even need to show up for the event?" ~ Rylee </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>Colton manipulates his way into her personal life, work life and lives of the boys in her care. <br>With his money and influence, Colton funds Corporate Cares project. With his help, the new facilities can now become a reality.<br>We see glimpses of Colton's sweet nature and how he interacts with the boys.<br><br><br>Rylee fights the pull between them. She knows Colton only wants one thing. <br>She pushes and pushes Colton. The banter between the two was fun and sexy to watch. <br>She really knows how to twist him in knots. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"Hi Ace," I say guardedly. "Since when did you add stalker to you repertoire of talents?" <br>He dashes me a lightening fast grin. "I'd be more than happy to show you my talents, Sweetheart."<br>I roll my eyes at him. "Womanising is not talent."~<br><br>~"Keep fighting me, Sweetheart. The feistier you are, the harder you make me."~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>The scene in the Club… OH GOD the sexual tension was seriously dripping off the pages! <br>I swear the whole thing had my heart beating fast, OH GOD what a build up.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571255090i/28304443.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"Well, thanks for the update.<br> I'll let you in on a little something as well, Ace. <br>I don't like being made to feel like I'm sloppy seconds to your bevy of babes.<br>You're developing a pattern of wanting me right after I know you've been with another. That's a habit you're going to need to break or nothing else is going to happen here."~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>And of course Rylee succumbs to the temptation of Colton. Even if for just one night. And when they do…. HOLY SMOKING HOT.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571255090i/28304444.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"I want to take my time with you, Rylee. I want to build you up nice and slow and sweet like you need. Push you to crash over that edge. And then I want to fuck you the way I need to. Fast and hard until you're screaming my name. The way I've wanted to since you fell out of that storage closet and into my life."~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420009ra/833069.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420009ra/833070.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>But once isn't enough for Colton. <br>Colton wants her, needs to consume her. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"You make me need Rylee," he whispers hoarsely as he takes one more step. <br>"And I don't ever need anything from anybody."~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>But only on his terms. <br>He is concealing some incredibly damaging experiences from his past which continues to haunt him. <br>He won't, can't do commitment. His history makes him test the limits of people to prove he's not worthy of their love. <br><br><br>But, Rylee can't be what he needs. <br>His way is the only way he knows how to be. And Rylee wants more than he is offering. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"I will not be inconsequential, Colton. To you or anyone else."~<br><br>~"I'm hardwired this way, Rylee. I'll purposely do something to hurt you to prove that I can. To prove that you won't stick around regardless off the consequences. To prove that I can control the situation. To control that I don't get hurt."~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>Everything about their relationship is so incredibly intense - the good, the bad, the sex, the drama. It's full on. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~ He is my fire on a cold night, the sun warming my skin on a cool spring morning, the wind caressing my face on an autumn day- he is everything that makes me feel alive, and whole, and beautiful, And desired.~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571255090i/28304445.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I loved the chemistry between them gosh, <b>these two were hot. </b><br>Even the scenes where they don't actually have sex were extremely HOT! <br>It was definitely one of those books were <i>'getting there' </i>was just as good as the act itself.<br><br>I felt their pain, I felt their anger and I felt the intensity of their love?? (Love, I'm not sure if it's love or lust? definitely the beginnings of love) <br>They both have troubled pasts and Rylee does open up about her past in this book.<br>Colton, has far more secrets and only a few are revealed in this instalment.<br><br>Rylee did it for me in this one. She knew what she wanted, as much as it hurt to not have Colton the way she wanted, she still refused to give into him when he couldn't give her what she needed. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>~"I deserve more than this, Colton." I whisper raising my eyes to meet his, "And so do you." <br>"I'm sorry I can't be what you want me to be.<br> Please take me home Colton." ~</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>I loved the writing, loved the characters and the storyline had me hooked, I was consumed with it every step of the way!<br><br>This was the first instalment of the Driven Trilogy, and does end in a cliffhanger…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1571255090i/28304446._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I know, I know.. <b>but</b> don't fret ladies, the wait isn't too far away… with the second instalment expected to be released in August this year. <br><br>An amazing Debut by K. Bromberg <br>She is the REAL DEAL!! <br><br>I can't wait for Rylee and Colton's story to continue. <br><br>+++ 5 STARS +++<br><br>Buy it.<br>Read it.<br>Love it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>ARC courtesy of author K. Bromberg in exchange for an honest review <br>Review will be posted @ <a href="http://www.fabfunandtantalizingreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Fab, Fun &amp; Tantalizing Reads </a></i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11752811934340307479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
